Five Academic Societies Joint Annual Meeting - Original Speech by Kong Xiangxi (Continued) 116

However, in what areas should you all engage in national construction to be effective? I have a few ideas to briefly contribute to you all.

1. Construction should be in line with China's national conditions. What are China's current national conditions? I believe you all already know. China today is a poor country, but it has vast land and abundant resources, clearly like a great treasure trove, but without the key to open it. Therefore, it can be said that China is poor but not truly poor. At the same time, it is also a weak country, but if China's four hundred million people can unite as one, then with everyone's will forming a fortress, it can also become a strong nation in the world. Therefore, it can also be said that China is weak but not truly weak. However, during this transitional period, if we plan to build up the country and restore its original strength, we must prescribe the right medicine. All construction must, first and foremost, be in line with the country's national conditions. Otherwise, we may bring in many things from foreign countries, and if we follow foreign conventions in everything, building everything in the same way, without considering our own financial resources, it would inevitably be ill-suited to the country's environment, and too far removed from the goal of saving the nation.

2. Construction should be in line with current needs. A country's construction has countless aspects, especially when China's industry is backward. To align with the national conditions, it is necessary to pre-determine an overall plan. During construction, we must weigh the importance and set a priority among what is urgent and what is not. For example, we may see a Western-style building and find it magnificent, but if a family of five builds a Western-style building that can house twenty people, this is not practical. Previously, when I was in Japan, I saw the rain shelters built at Tokyo Station in Japan, which were very simple. The top was just a sheet of galvanized iron, and the bottom was just a few rough wooden posts. However, when it rained heavily, it could still provide shelter. Although it didn't cost much, it was still their own. Looking back at our country, when we arrive in Beiping, as soon as we get to the East Station, we see a very grand rain shelter, which feels very impressive, but it cost a lot of money, and it was all borrowed from foreign countries. So, as a result, the money earned by the railway can only be used to repay debts and cannot be used for development and improvement. In China in the past, there were countless situations like this. Therefore, I feel that people in the engineering field, in particular, should pay attention to this.

3. Construction should be within our own capabilities. Traditionally, Chinese scholars often read dead books and were inflexible. Today's students studying abroad also inevitably make this mistake. Whatever they learn abroad, they use it entirely upon returning home. All the materials are bought from foreign countries. Not to mention that the annual outflow of money is very large, it is also a great pity that China's original raw materials are not researched and utilized. Now, construction must try to find domestic raw materials as much as possible, which not only aligns with the principles of the national economy but also yields practical uses. For example, the vegetable oil lamps used in China in the past had very small flames. After improvements, kerosene was used for lighting, which increased the flame. However, the glass covers of kerosene lamps are easily broken if one is not careful. Therefore, economical families do not use lamp covers. As a result, many poor families in Shanxi use lamps without glass covers, and later, many people developed groin sores due to kerosene poisoning. Only after medical research was this discovered. Therefore, when I was in the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, I told their technical personnel to research and remodel vegetable oil lamps with glass covers, which would not only prevent the outflow of profits but also be harmless to the body. Later, indeed, Mr. Zhong and Xiao Hechang successfully experimented after a certain degree of testing. A few months ago, Mr. Xiao brought it to show me, and I was very happy to see that the light was very good. This is also a significant contribution to society. Also, China's medicinal materials have their own special strengths, but when they are eaten, even the residue is swallowed. In these areas, if we can conduct research and improve them, extract the residue and refine the essence, they would be just as fine as foreign medicines. Not only could they treat sick people, but they could also sustain the livelihoods of many people who collect and sell medicine, and reduce much outflow of money. For example, ephedrine and garlic essence are praised and readily adopted by foreigners. In my opinion, science only has ancient and modern, not Chinese and foreign. As long as we can integrate the old and new and connect everything, we will surely have great inventions. Today, it is a very good phenomenon that five academic societies can jointly hold an annual meeting, because Chinese people have always been self-centered and separate. Especially in academic fields, there are various systems and factions. Since ancient times, academic societies have either attacked each other or pointed fingers at each other. But today, there are societies like the Chinese Institute of Chemical Engineers and the Chinese Institute of Electrical Engineering, etc., that can unite together, be affectionate, and learn from each other. This is a very good phenomenon in Chinese academia. Originally, to do things, we must cooperate with each other, unite as one, and then we can achieve excellent results. For example, to build a house, the architect makes the design, the sanitary engineer installs sanitary equipment, and the civil engineer collects materials and hires labor. Only through mutual cooperation can this house be built. However, Chinese people have traditionally lacked this spirit of cooperation. Today, I am very pleased to see this good spirit. I hope you all will continue to work hard, continue to explore, and move forward together on the path of invention. I also feel that it is not impossible to take the strengths of others and discard our own weaknesses. Even if what China has invented over the past few decades is no longer very applicable, we can take the strengths of others, discard our own weaknesses, and strive to improve. This is also the path we should take. After studying other people's things, we can imitate them. Although we cannot catch up with them head-on, we can still be on par with them. Japan is the most capable of imitation. Now, when we look at the things invented in Japan, some may even surpass Europe and the United States. Things that Europe and the United States do not have may be invented in Japan. The United States is a scientifically advanced country, but Japanese goods are commonly seen in one or two-cent shops. Also, India is a British colony, but Japanese cloth can sell well in India. Furthermore, Lancashire and Manchester in England are the centers of the British cotton industry, and some say that the outer garments worn by the workers in the cotton mills are also Japanese goods. Although I have never seen it, it is said that this is indeed the case. We may ask, where does Japan's long-term progress come from? It comes from imitation. Being able to imitate others and promote the new by discarding the old is what has enabled Japan's industry to make such long-term progress. Therefore, I feel that although China may not be able to invent many things, it can also study and imitate the things invented by others. In addition to imitation, we must also improve. "To do a good job, one must first sharpen one's tools." When I was the Minister of Industry, I planned to try to establish a central machine factory to improve the machines used in Chinese handicrafts so that women in Chinese families could use these improved things to develop China's household industry. I think that you all sitting here today must have the same feelings as me, and I hope everyone will work hard as much as possible, because construction work can only be started from agriculture, industry, and commerce. Now, our country's exports are decreasing day by day, and our imports are increasing day by day, resulting in a huge trade deficit year after year, which has plunged the country into poverty. Now, if everyone wants to engage in construction, they must find ways to help agriculture, industry, and commerce. If we want to help agriculture, industry, and commerce, we must reduce imports and increase exports. Based on the points I just mentioned, I cannot help but have three hopes: In addition to invention, I also hope that we can imitate imported goods as much as possible and improve exported goods as much as possible. Then our country's raw materials can naturally be utilized, and our country's foreign trade can gradually develop. At the same time, we must pay attention to the conservation of financial and material resources, and make everything in line with economic principles, which would greatly benefit the national economy and the people's livelihood. I have said that saving the country does not necessarily mean becoming an official in the political arena to save the country. In fact, what is most important and most closely related to the country is not officials but inventors. If you can all concentrate on inventing various weapons of national defense, especially in the current critical situation of the country, it will be of great need and great help. Looking around the world, military weapons are changing with each passing day. This is the result of scientists racking their brains and burying themselves in hard work. But in China, nothing like this has been heard. Therefore, today I would like to reiterate this point and ask you all to pay more attention to it. Do not let the Qi Lu people who invented the breech-loading rifle be the only ones to be praised. However, invention must be done by people with considerable knowledge in order to achieve results. Among China's four hundred million people, I only hope that you all sitting here today, because you have considerable knowledge and considerable experience, and you also have considerable status in society. If everyone can consistently strengthen our will and embrace the spirit of hard work, hard work, and practical work, I believe that we will make a very great contribution to the country. Therefore, today, in my busy schedule, I took the time to participate in this grand meeting and contribute these few ideas. I hope everyone will pay attention to them. Although I spoke casually, it was entirely out of sincerity. I hope everyone can accept them and put them into practice. This would be of great help to our current nation and people, and it is also the greatest mission of this conference.

Second Term of Smoker Licenses - Deadline for Renewal at the End of the Month 117

Only Over Ten Thousand People Have Renewed Their Licenses

The Inspection Team Is Intensifying Its Efforts to Investigate

According to the Public Security Bureau's announcement, the reporting of opium addiction in this city began on the 10th of this month. According to the person in charge of the Bureau's Smoker Registration Section, the reporting of opium addiction starts with propaganda and investigation. Recently, a propaganda team has been organized to go out and give lectures every day, so those who register as smokers and request to quit opium addiction are very enthusiastic. From the start of reporting to May 23rd, the number of people applying for ordinary licenses was 775, the number of people registering for poor people's licenses was 1164, and the number of people requesting to quit smoking was 358. There are still a large number of registered smokers who have not renewed their licenses. Unable to Bear the Pain, He Cried Out - Ye Haisheng Described as Increasingly Weak - He Miserably Confessed to Being Framed 119

Ye Swallowed Keys and Copper Buttons in Prison to Commit Suicide, But Both Times He Did Not Die - He Admitted to the Murder of Japanese Soldiers Because He Could Not Bear the Torture - The Judge Ordered Ye to Be Sent to the Municipal Council Hospital for Treatment

The gun assassination of Japanese naval fleet soldier Nakayama Hideo stationed in Shanghai, for which the city authorities offered a reward for the arrest of the murderer, has been ongoing for half a year. Recently, the Public Concession Police successively arrested Cantonese Ye Haisheng (nickname Xiao Guangdong), Yang Wendao, and Zhou Sherong, and filed a public prosecution against them for murder. After repeated trials by the First Special District Court's collegial panel, Ye Haisheng repeatedly confessed that he shot the sailor, except that Yang and Zhou have not confessed. However, his confession was bizarre. For the sake of prudence, the presiding judge, Mr. Xiao Xiefei, ordered the police to escort Ye Haisheng and invited the Municipal Council's lawyer and the defendant's defense lawyer last Friday to personally go to the

Scene of the Incident

Area of Hongkou Binle'an Road to investigate and order Ye to demonstrate the situation of the shooting that day, in order to find the truth. The Municipal Government, the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and the Japanese military headquarters sent secretaries, section chiefs, armed military officers and soldiers to the court to observe. In addition, because the court's restrictions were very strict and arbitrary entry and exit were not allowed, there were only a few dozen people in the audience, so the courtroom did not feel crowded. However, the defendant Ye Haisheng's appearance was

Increasingly Weak

The detectives escorted Ye, along with Yang Wendao and Zhou Sherong, to the court and stood behind the defendant's dock, looking very listless. The lawyer Zhang Zhirang, who was appointed by the court to defend Ye, requested permission to present the results of the previous inspection with the judge before the start of the interrogation, regarding the two questions of the bullet and pistol found by the police at the scene. The court nodded in agreement. Lawyer Zhang then said that the police believed that the particle was the one that killed the Japanese sailor, but Ye Haisheng demonstrated the shooting situation that day, the deceased was facing north from the south, and Ye followed him. All Directors and Supervisors Personally Presided Over Affairs at the Market Yesterday

The Shanghai Fish Market of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce recently experienced a market strike by vendors from various districts due to a small number of individuals obstructing business over transportation issues. Following earnest persuasion from the market, a partial resumption of business was achieved yesterday morning. However, a small number of people continued to obstruct operations. Yesterday, all directors and supervisors of the market personally went to the market to oversee the situation and mediate the dispute. A complete resolution was reached last night, and all fish vendors resumed business this morning. Details are as follows:

Emergency Meeting of Directors and Supervisors Yesterday

Following the occurrence of the fish vendors' dispute, and the market's explanations, the Tanhuhu Lianyi Association notified all fish vendors to resume business as usual yesterday morning. However, some individuals continued to cause trouble, resulting in obstruction. Incidents of vendors being stopped and beaten occurred, but were suppressed by the police. The Fish Market Board of Directors held an emergency joint meeting of all directors and supervisors at the Board of Directors' office in the Zhonghui Building yesterday morning at 9:00 AM to discuss solutions. Attendees included Chairman Du Yuesheng, Standing Directors Tang Chengzong, Gui Yanfang, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Shenzhi, Yu Zuoting, as well as Market Manager Wang Xiaolai, and Deputy Managers Zhu Kaiguan and Sun Guchen. After the meeting concluded at 10:00 AM, all attending directors, supervisors, the manager and deputy managers went to the fish market at 11:00 AM to personally oversee the situation and prevent further disruptions. They remained until 5:00 PM.

Full Resumption of Business by Fish Vendors Citywide This Morning

Following the unfortunate events after business yesterday morning, the dispute has been completely resolved after repeated persuasion by the market. It is now understood that all fish vendors in the city will resume business as usual this morning. Market officials contacted many vendors regarding all issues as of last night, and all have come to an understanding, so there should be no further problems. Fish caught by fishermen during the market strike, which could not be sold, can also be completely sold off starting today.

Vendor Representatives from Various Districts Petitioned Yesterday Morning

Vendors from various districts of the city have been cooperating and trading smoothly since the opening of the fish market. The unfortunate incident that occurred recently is deeply regrettable. To resolve misunderstandings, representatives including Wang Yuanzhou, He Linsheng, Zhang Liling, Xu Shiming, Li Yulou, and others, were dispatched to the Fish Market Board of Directors yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM to petition, expressing their support for the market. They will also dispatch a large number of representatives to the market today to persuade vendors and prevent uninformed individuals from being taken advantage of.

Public Works Department Fire Brigade Implements Staff Reduction 122

Senior Staff Given Retirement Pensions

Remaining Staff Dismissed Based on Seniority

Regarding the Public Works Department Fire Brigade's budget reduction, the Public Works Department directors Carnay, Qielili, and Zhuo Jiang formed a subcommittee to investigate improvements to the Fire Brigade's organization and finances. It is now heard that the subcommittee has recently reported to the directors, indicating that the Fire Brigade's development has indeed exceeded what is necessary for public safety. Therefore, staff reductions of both Chinese and foreign personnel are unavoidable. The subcommittee's recommendation regarding personnel reductions has also been carefully considered by the Public Works Department's Personnel Committee, which has established a plan. It has been found that three long-serving staff members in the Fire Brigade's headquarters are being dismissed. It is proposed that they be given retirement pensions based on their respective ages and years of service. Junior staff may be transferred to other Public Works Department offices or given severance pay based on their years of service. All dismissed staff will receive their full retirement savings. Furthermore, according to the subcommittee's recommendation, the three Fire Brigade lookout towers that were previously decided to be retained will now be staffed entirely by Chinese personnel. All foreign lookout tower staff will be dismissed. In addition to receiving their full retirement savings, these dismissed staff will also be entitled to severance pay and government-funded repatriation. Chinese junior staff without employment contracts will be given their full retirement savings, severance pay, and one month's salary, and may also be repatriated. The subcommittee believes that the aforementioned staff reduction plan will not affect the Fire Brigade's operational efficiency. Therefore, the directors have resolved to adopt the subcommittee's recommendations and plan to implement them in the near future.

Iron Ball Turns Out to Be a Bomb - Explodes After Being Hammered 123

Zhu the Dwarf Seriously Injured

Zhu the Dwarf, a local resident aged 61, works as a boatman ferrying goods between Pudong and Puxi. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, he transported nine steel bars from Pudong and was preparing to unload them near the Zhapu Road Bridge when he suddenly spotted an iron ball at the bottom of the boat. Not knowing what it was, he hammered it with an iron mallet. Unexpectedly, the ball was a bomb, and it exploded upon impact with a loud bang. Iron fragments flew in all directions, and Zhu the Dwarf was hit head-on, causing severe head injuries with exposed flesh and blood. Nearby police officers were notified and immediately reported to the police station, which dispatched a vehicle to take him to the hospital for treatment.

Abnormal Temperature in May This Year 124

Due to Excessively High Atmospheric Pressure

According to the Shanghai Times, the temperature in the city has dropped sharply in the past two or three days. Last Friday, the 5th, it was 79.7 degrees, while this Tuesday, the highest was only 66 degrees. According to the Zikawei Observatory, such cool weather in Shanghai in May is unprecedented in recent years. The reason is due to unusually high atmospheric pressure in the area, causing air to rise, while Siberian winds take the opportunity to invade from the northwest. In previous years at this time, Siberian air would have advanced eastward, but this year, due to the high pressure in China, it has turned southeast. As for why the atmospheric pressure is unusually high, the reason cannot be stated, and the observatory does not want to attribute it to sunspots or other similar phenomena. The observatory compared the temperature from May 1st to 26th this year with the same period last year. The average maximum temperature for the 26 days this year was slightly less than 70 degrees, while it was 85 degrees last year, a difference of more than 15 degrees, which is enough to indicate the abnormal temperature in Shanghai in May this year. The observatory also expects the temperature to increase gradually in the future, rather than changing suddenly.

More than one hundred trade associations in this city, including the machine dyeing and weaving industry, sugar industry, tea industry, domestic rubber products industry, north-south goods brokerage industry, medicinal materials industry, fruit and local goods industry, new medicine industry, pharmaceutical factory industry, travel industry, local goods industry, biscuit, candy, canned food and bread industry, silk and satin printing industry, iron printing and can industry, thermos bottle manufacturing industry, cattle and sheep raw leather industry, fur, oil and bone industry, electrical appliance industry, freight car industry, simple book industry, pawnshop industry, shoe leather nail last industry, tree firewood industry, fresh pork slaughtering industry, fresh pork selling industry, duck slaughtering industry, wood industry, flower industry, Lu Sun industry, woolen factory industry, redwood dismantling industry, seafood grocery industry, lumber industry, western paint industry, silk dyeing workshop industry, glass industry, knitting industry, napping industry, refining industry, etc., issued a joint statement yesterday regarding the attacks against Wang Xiaolai: Recently, a so-called Federation of Industry and Commerce has printed and distributed leaflets slandering Mr. Wang Xiaolai, the former Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the current consultant to the Chamber of Commerce. According to the Yongli Factory listed on the leaflet, it is a member of the Rubber Industry Association, the Samsung Factory and Shunfeng Factory are members of the Machine Dyeing and Weaving Industry Association, the Xiefengsheng Pharmacy is a member of the Medicinal Materials Industry Association, Gong Fanglai is a member of the North-South Goods Brokerage Industry Association, and Guangyuan Sugar Firm is a member of the Sugar Industry Association. All of these are completely untrue. The false accusations are often made by unscrupulous people who forge names, engrave needles privately, and have ulterior motives. Mr. Wang Xiaolai has led the Chamber of Commerce for many years with fairness and integrity. Chinese and foreign merchants and public opinion are united. The rumors do not harm him in the slightest. However, the associations are all legitimate merchant organizations in this city, and it is difficult for us to remain silent in the face of this malicious attack. Therefore, we issue this joint statement, hoping that it will be noted.

New Invention: Free Light Bulb Factory Established 137

One Bulb Can Be Used for Five Purposes

Ministry of Industry Approves Patent

Recently, Chinese people have been making new and wonderful inventions in industry. Recently, Mr. Bao has invented a free light bulb whose light can be changed at will, and Mr. Yu Weiqing has independently established a Qite Light Bulb Factory to manufacture it. Yesterday, the factory officially opened and invited reporters to visit in the morning. The factory is located at No. 457, North Henan Road. According to the inventor Mr. Bao, he was originally a worker at the power company, but in his spare time, he was able to study the electrical business carefully. Because he felt that the brightness of the light bulb could not be freely adjusted, he started the motivation for research and improvement. After about two years of trial and error, he succeeded and created two sample bulbs, which were submitted to the Ministry of Industry and approved for a five-year patent under the Ministry of Industry's No. 1324. Now, Mr. Su Yu Weiqing has invested in setting up a factory to manufacture it. From the beginning of preparation to the present, it has been more than half a year. After many researches and improvements, and months of field tests, it can be officially shipped. In addition to manufacturing patented light bulbs, it also manufactures ordinary single-use light bulbs to meet the needs of society, etc. This kind of light bulb has three kinds. One is called the Qi character bulb, which contains three light wires of different brightness. The first wire is 5 candlepower, the second wire is 25 candlepower, and the third wire is 15 candlepower. The change of brightness completely depends on the spring part inside the specially made copper head. From the surface, it is no different from the copper head of an ordinary light bulb. In fact, its structure is divided into two layers, inner and outer. The copper head is installed on the glass shell and tightly attached inside the outer copper head. The structure of the spring part is extremely complex. When using it, the user only needs to press the glass shell with one hand and rotate it slightly. The first wire of 5 candlepower will light up alone. Continue to rotate, the second wire and the first wire will light up at the same time, adding up to 20 candlepower. Then turn to the second wire to light up alone, which is 25 candlepower. Then the third wire and the second wire will light up at the same time, adding up to 40 candlepower. The third wire lights up alone, which is 15 candlepower. Another turn can automatically extinguish it without having to turn on or off the switch. And you can turn left or right as you like, without the risk of electric shock or explosion. So with only one bulb, you can use it as five. Ordinary families need it the most. There is also a special character bulb with three filaments inside, all of the same brightness. Adjacent filaments cannot light up at the same time. The structure of the copper head is the same as the Qi character bulb. When the first filament inside is damaged, you only need to press the glass shell with your hand and rotate it slightly. The first filament can still light up. After the first filament breaks, the third filament can still be used. Therefore, the use time of this light bulb is no different from that of three ordinary light bulbs. Factories, schools, stores and other institutions can save the trouble of replacing light bulbs when they use this kind of light bulb. It is the most economical and suitable. As for the style of the glass shell, in addition to the ordinary round bulb, there is also a new type of flat round bulb. This kind of light bulb emits light in all directions, and there is absolutely no drawback of consuming light. The style is beautiful and completely different from ordinary light bulbs. It is really an unprecedented creation in the light bulb industry.

Shanghai Telephone Company Issues Supplementary Remarks 138

The Shanghai Telephone Company issued a statement on May 24th, the purpose of which was to make telephone users more aware of telephone services. However, a few points in it have caused misunderstandings, and it seems necessary to explain them. The Shanghai Telephone Company's work report for the previous year was sent to the工部局 (Gōngbù jú, an administrative organ during the concession era) and published. It mentioned that in 1935, it suffered losses due to the influence of the market. In January and February of this year, it still suffered losses. However, since March 1st, the number of users has increased by several thousands due to the implementation of the new price rate calculated by the number of calls. From April to now, the number of telephone users has continued to increase. Therefore, the Shanghai Telephone Company firmly believes that its users know that the new price rate is not a burden, but can obtain higher value. A little more explanation can also be given regarding the telephone book. All basic records are registered in the English telephone book. What is contained in the Chinese telephone book is only for the convenience of Chinese users for reference. Therefore, in the currently published Chinese telephone book, all unnecessary records and names have been deleted in order to make the cost more economical and not lose its original value, and to make it more convenient for those who use the Chinese telephone book. From this point of view, it is indeed wrong to determine the amount of business of the Shanghai Telephone Company based on the number of telephone books. In short, since March 1st of this year, people from all walks of life have become increasingly aware of telephone services, and therefore the number of people installing telephones has also increased day by day.

Shanghai's Paint Industry (Continued) 148

— Chief Editor, China Credit

(An Overview of Shanghai's Industry and Commerce, No. 26)

(4) Types of Paint: Paint types vary depending on their purpose, with distinctions for protecting gold, wood, and earth. Due to the numerous names and differences in volume and color, it is difficult for those unfamiliar with the industry to understand them. A summary is as follows:

Paint: Divided into white and colored varieties. White paint is graded into six levels: 4A, 3A (or Super Superior), Double A, A, B, and C. Colored paint is graded into three levels: 3A, Double A, and A. 4A is the highest quality, descending in order. Housing, ships, and railways use a considerable amount, with gray paint being particularly popular. B and C grade paints are of lower quality and are only used as a primer (base coat). Sold by the "can" (喊), with each can divided into four small iron boxes, each box containing 28 pounds.

Ready-Mixed Paint: Divided into glossy and matte varieties, with grades of 3A and Double A. Used for high-end products and advertising signs. Measured in gallons. Apart from the five-gallon iron containers, one-gallon, half-gallon, and 2.5-gallon sizes are packaged in printed tin cans.

Enamel Paint: Similar in effect to varnish, suitable for coating both wood and iron items. Packaged in small, printed round cans, available in one-pound and half-pound sizes.

Red Lead Anti-Rust Paint: Specifically for use on roofs, bridges, ships, and ironware, with a rust-preventative effect, hence the name. Measured by the barrel, each barrel containing 56 pounds.

Varnish: Made by dissolving resins into a liquid. When applied to the surface of an object, it produces a sheen when dry. Therefore, it is commonly used on chairs, tables, wood, tin cans, labels, etc. Due to the different raw materials used, it is classified into types such as Amber Varnish, Kauri Varnish, Dammar Varnish, Sandarac Varnish, and Mastic Varnish.

(5) Paint Business Operations: The peak months for the paint business are spring and autumn, while summer and winter are slow months. The progress or decline of the business is tied to the prosperity of industries. In recent years, the real estate market has declined, and construction has stagnated, making it difficult for the industry to develop. The annual turnover of each factory ranges from over 800,000 yuan to as little as just over 100,000 yuan. Sales are primarily conducted through agents, who are paid commissions. Agents are stationed in various ports, and when goods are needed, they can directly purchase from the factory, with payment made after the goods are shipped and packed. There are also agencies in the Nanyang Islands, such as Zhen He in Singapore, Ying Hua in Batavia, and Hua Feng Tai in San Bin, all of which are sales outlets for Shanghai paints. The largest consumers of paint, such as shipyards and railways, use a bidding system, which creates competition among businesses. Construction companies mostly obtain their supplies through hardware stores, with few direct transactions. Foreign companies operating paint businesses in Shanghai include Jiu Ji, Xuan Qiao, Ji Xing, Hong Shou, Heng Da, Mei He, and Ruixiang Foreign Firm, among others, with Ji Xing having the largest scope, with annual sales reaching one million yuan. Local Anhui paint shops also act as sales agents. According to a survey from the 24th year of the Republic (1935), seven Chinese paint factories sold approximately 22,684,123 pounds of paint and approximately 301,641 gallons of varnish. The business index for recent years is as follows (using 1930 as the base year):

(6) Paint Sales and Imports: Paint sales are concentrated in urban areas, with very little use in remote rural areas. Shanghai, as a major commercial port with numerous tall buildings, has the highest demand and prefers high-quality products. However, due to various factors, the sales volume of domestic products is still lower than that of foreign products. However, in places such as Hankou, Sichuan, Qingdao, Fujian, and Guangdong, domestically produced paint can still occupy a considerable advantage. According to expert estimates, the ratio of domestic to foreign paint sales in Shanghai is 3:7, while in other domestic ports, it is the opposite. The three northeastern provinces were originally a region of high paint sales, but after the September 18th Incident (Mukden Incident), they have disappeared from the market. The Nanyang region is the only export destination for our country's paint, but it has recently been affected by the dumping of Japanese goods, leading to a significant decline.

The annual value of imported foreign paint is approximately one million Customs Gold Units. Imports from the United Kingdom are the most significant, followed by the United States, and then Japan. In terms of imported types, the United Kingdom mainly imports thick paint, the United States mainly imports varnish, and Japan mainly imports enamel paint. For the 24th year of the Republic (1935), the total import value was 817,777 Customs Gold Units, of which British goods accounted for 213,591, American goods accounted for 186,863, and Japanese goods accounted for 103,545. The ports of entry with the highest import volumes were Shanghai, Tianjin, and Guangzhou. In the 24th year, 551,273 Customs Gold Units were imported into Shanghai, 71,493 Customs Gold Units were imported into Tianjin, and 40,907 Customs Gold Units were imported into Guangzhou. The import values for the past two years are listed below (in Customs Gold Units):

Track and Field Training Class: Competition in Tianjin Yesterday; Three National Records Broken 149

Wang Shilin's Long Jump...7.03 Meters...Breaks National Record

Liu Furun's Shot Put...12.95 Meters...Breaks Far Eastern Record

Guo Jie's Discus...41.07 Meters...Breaks National Record

Tianjin, 27th - Athletes from the World Games Track and Field Training Class competed against top athletes from the Tianjin All-Sports Meet today. Guo Jie's discus throw of 41.07 meters also broke the national record. All were excellent results.

Detailed Record of the Competition Between the Training Class and Beijing City: Chen Baoqiu Breaks Another Far Eastern Record; Discus and 1500 Meters Also Set National Records 150

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The athletes from our country's World Games Track and Field Training Class and basketball team have gained a lot at Tsinghua University, and their results are outstanding. The Beiping City Spring Games were held for three days at the end of the training class. The results were also excellent among the provinces and cities in North China. Therefore, the top three in the Spring Games were selected as representatives of the Beiping team and agreed to compete against the World Games athletes at the Beiping Xian Nong Tan Public Stadium at 2 PM on the 25th. As a result, Chen Binqiu's shot put broke the Far Eastern record again. Guo Jie and Ma Wenbin's discus throws set new national records. Jia Lianren's 1500 meters also broke the national record. Peng Yongxin's javelin throw equaled the national record. The basketball performance was dispersed after only one game due to spectators rushing into the arena. A detailed record of the grand occasion and results is as follows:

Track and Field Sketches 151

Zhao Bingheng First in 100 Meters

The 100-meter race was held first. Liu Changchun was unable to compete due to a foot ailment that required rest. The participants from the World Games training class were Zhao Bingheng and Fu Baolu. The representatives from Beiping were Yan Zhaoshen, Yang Haipeng, and Wang Qiang, for a total of five people. At the start, Yan Zhaoshen took the lead. Zhao Bingheng was at the back for the first 20 meters. Zhao then charged forward at 30 meters, leading the way. He finished in one breath, about a meter ahead of Yan at the finish line. The time was 11.1 seconds. Zhao Bingheng's start was a bit slow, and his final sprint was also a bit weak. He needs to work on pushing his chest forward. However, his speed is indeed comparable to Liu Changchun. His running stride and swing are both excellent. If he can further study the start and finish, a time of 10.7 or 10.8 seconds is not difficult to achieve. Yan Zhaoshen's original name was Yan Chengtian. Although he is a newcomer in Tianjin with Han Jinglin and Yang Bozhong, he is also a promising talent.

200 Meters Dai Shu Guo Champion

The 200-meter race started at 4 PM. Three people participated. The course was a straight line. Zhao Bingheng did not participate because he felt a bit tired after the 100-meter race. Dai Shuguo made a guest appearance (Dai originally specialized in the 400 meters). Dai also fell behind at the start. After about 40 meters, Dai had already moved two steps ahead. The others could only see his dust and follow behind. He was about four feet away from the second place at the finish line. Xiao Dai's body is a bit thin, so it may not be suitable for him to train in the 400 meters. However, his upper body swing in the 200 meters is not quite right, so it slightly affected the result. However, his running the 200 meters was ultimately a guest appearance, so we should not be too demanding.

Two Competitors in the 400 Meters

There were only two participants in the 400 meters: Li Shiming from the World Games training class and Zhang Yinglong from the Beiping city team. It was a pity that Dai Shuguo could not compete at the same time. After 50 meters, Li was leading by about seven or eight meters. At the finish line, the time was 53.3 seconds. The second place, Zhang Yinglong, had a time of 57.6 seconds. Li's running style in the first stage was still good. His calf movements are not yet perfect, and his waist straightening needs to be trained.

1500 Meters Breaks National Record

The 1500-meter race started at 3 PM. Only Jia Lianren and Du Huaju participated. Du Huaju initially followed about two meters behind Jia. After 400 meters, Du gradually became exhausted and fell behind by about ten meters. Jia continued to work hard and ran freely. At the 1100-meter mark, Jia was about 100 meters ahead of Du, with a time of 3 minutes 7 seconds. Before long, the entire course was about to be completed. Jia further increased his speed in the last 100 meters, using his final sprint. His time was 4 minutes 20 seconds. Although it was slightly slower than the previous record of 4 minutes 13 seconds, it still broke the national record. The second place, Du Huaju's time, was 4 minutes 53 seconds. Jia's expression was normal after the race, without any sign of exhaustion, which was already commendable. His tall and solid physique did not seem like that of a middle-distance runner.

High Hurdles Shaozhou Wins Nationally

Three people participated in the 110-meter high hurdles: Lin Shaozhou, Huang Ying傺, and Yang Daochong. They competed at 2 PM, after the 100-meter race. Lin and Huang's results were similar, and the competition was fierce and very interesting. Initially, the three were parallel. By the third hurdle, Yang Daochong had fallen behind by about a meter. It was difficult to distinguish between Lin and Huang. They were almost the same. The entire course was completed, with Lin and Huang separated by only one shoulder. The time was 16 seconds. Lin Shaozhou's high hurdle posture is very good, but his waist is slightly bent when he lowers. Huang's hurdle crossing is worse, but his speed is still commendable.

1600 Meter Relay Beiping Falls Behind

The 1600-meter relay training class athletes were Jia Lianren, Dong Hanwen, Li Shiming, and Dai Shuguo. The Beiping representatives were Wu Bin, Zhang Jiming, Du Huaju, and Yan Zhaoshen. In the first leg, Jia Lianren ran ahead by more than 20 meters. There was little progress in the second leg. In the third leg, the Beiping representatives had fallen behind by more than 100 meters. Dai Shuguo held the baton and rushed forward in the fourth leg. When he reached the finish line, he was about 150 meters ahead of the Beiping representatives. The time was 5 minutes 1 second. The training class athletes' baton passing was still poor. If Liu Changchun could replace Dong Hanwen, the result would be even more impressive, because Dong has not been focusing on the 400 meters for a long time.

Track and Field Sketches

Chen Baoqiu Breaks the Far Eastern Record Twice

The participants in this event were Chen Baoqiu and Guo Jie from the training class, and Tian Jingyao and Cui Xiangkang from Beiping. Each person threw six times. Chen Baoqiu's initial throw was 12 meters. Guo Jie was only 10 meters. Tian Jingyao was 9 meters. Cui Xiangkang was behind them. In the second throw, Tian Jingyao defeated Guo Jie. Chen Baoqiu had reached 12.98 meters. Finally, the Iron Bull shouted and threw 13.26 meters, breaking the Far Eastern record. The previous Far Eastern record holder was the Japanese athlete Abe Isao, with a result of 12.905 meters. Tian Jingyao was 11.41 meters. Guo Jie was 11.3 meters. Cui Xiangkang was 10.64 meters. Chen's one time breaking the Far Eastern record was at the last test at Tsinghua.

Javelin Peng Yongxin Equals National Record

Da Peng worked hard because he failed the test in Tsinghua, and he also failed at the Spring Games a few days ago. He used an injection of stimulant. On the 25th, the weather was good, and there was no headwind, so he could perform at his best. Zhou Changxing also did not show weakness and closely followed him. Peng achieved a national record of 50.56 meters on the third throw. Changxing's result was 49.65 meters, in second place. Third and fourth were Li Shiming and Bi Huaxuan from Beiping.

Guo Jie Breaks National Discus Record Twice

The discus results were also a great achievement. Guo Jie set a new record of 39.62 meters at the fifth test a few days ago. Yesterday, his release was very stable and his posture was reasonable. He did not have the problem of focusing too much on one side. When he reached 41.13 meters, he not only broke the national record of 37.85 meters held by Leng Peigen, but also exceeded his result from the fifth test. Ma Wenbin's strength was weaker, but it was also amazing. He broke the national record with a result of 38.50 meters.

Fu Baolu's Pole Breaks Again

After the long-awaited pole vault appeared, the entire stadium cheered. The starting height was 2.90 meters. Fu jumped over it in one leap, and his posture was beautiful, exciting the audience. Zhan Yiyuan's first attempt was unsuccessful. Xu Shoupeng imitated him. Zhan and Xu barely crossed the bar on the second attempt and barely overcame the difficulty. They then raised it to 3.05 meters and then to 3.71 meters. Baolu jumped over them all. Zhan and Xu failed on three attempts. The pole broke when it was released because the distance between the pole and the pole rack was too close. At 3.73 inches, Fu jumped over again twice. Because only Fu was pole vaulting, and the pole he used was cracked due to the dry weather and could not be used, he could not show his skills. Head coach John Ma stopped him because he was afraid of being too tired. The item that everyone was watching came to an end.

Liu Mengjiu's High Jump Approaches National Record

Wu Bixian from the High Jump Competition Training Class did not appear in Tianjin. Liu Mengjiu attended. Liu overwhelmed the famous Beiping player Jin Yan at the 16th North China Games and became famous. Several years have passed, and the record is still there. Wang Shilin also did not participate. Zhou Changxing accompanied him to participate. Yang Xiangsun and Zhang Shutian from the Normal University of Beiping appeared. They started jumping from 1.60 meters. The bar gradually increased, and gradually eliminated. Later, because the sandpit was not loose enough, the venue was moved to a better location for another competition. Raised to 1.8 meters, which is close to Wu Bixian's national record (1.83 meters). Liu leaped over it three times and exhausted his strength. If the bar is raised again, he did not create a new record. Zhou Changxing used too much force in throwing the javelin and became crossbow arrows. He retreated to fourth place. Yang and Zhang were ranked second and third.

Liu Changchun Talks

More than 20 people from our country's World Games Track and Field Training Class, including Jia Lianren, Huang Yingjie, Liu Changchun, Fu Baolu, Guo Jie, and Lin Shaozhou, were invited by Beiping Mayor Qin Dechun to a luncheon at the city government's assembly hall at 12 noon on the 26th. The athletes took two large cars from Tsinghua University to the city for the banquet. All the officials from the Spring Games accompanied them, and Li Zhou, the sports supervisor of the Social Bureau, Le Yongnian, the director of the middle school department, and Wang Lan, a veteran of the sports world, were responsible for the reception. Mayor Qin Dechun personally attended and gave a speech. The banquet was very lively. They all dispersed happily around 2 PM. After the banquet, all the athletes took cars to the East Station and took the train to Tianjin at 3:35 PM. They stayed at the Tianjin YMCA. They had a friendly match with British athletes in Tianjin on the 27th. After the game, they took the train south and are expected to arrive in Shanghai on the 29th. According to team leader Liu Changchun, the entire team plans to compete against Western foreigners in Shanghai and will sail overseas on June 26th. The team has been training in Ping for more than a month, and many national records have been broken. Fu Baolu's pole vault broke the Far Eastern record, with a result of 4.015 meters, breaking the 4-meter record held by Japanese athlete Nishi Yu at the Far Eastern Games. Chen Baoqiu's shot put broke the Far Eastern record twice. The first decision was at the final test of the training class, with a result of 12.975 meters, breaking the 12.905 record held by Akiyama Akira at the Far Eastern Games today. The second was on the 25th, that is, the training class athletes competed against the top three in the Beiping Spring Games. Chen broke Akiyama's highest record again with a result of 13.263, further achieving good results. Although Fu and Chen's results may not win the championship at the World Games, Fu's pole vault, if using a good pole and with further training, is not far from the world record, and may be able to show some talent in Berlin, to wash away the shame of our Chinese nation's sick man. As for the representatives to Germany, it has not yet been determined, and it will be determined after the preliminaries in Shanghai. For this preliminary election in Shanghai, attention must also be paid to the sportsmanship of the athletes, because international competitions are different from domestic competitions. A moment of carelessness is related to the national face, so it is not easy to talk about who in the training class can go abroad at this moment, but Fu and Chen are quite confident, and he himself is getting old and unable to do anything, and his leg disease has not healed, so he is afraid that he will not be selected.

Notice to Members of the Sports Delegation to Germany 152

The China National Amateur Athletic Federation has formulated the following guidelines for members of the Sports Delegation to Germany:

Organization Name: The delegation is named the Sports Delegation to Germany. All personnel going to Germany for inspection, whether recommended by the Ministry of Education, selected and subsidized by the Federation, or self-funded and approved by the Federation, are members of the delegation.

Itinerary and Dates: A. The delegation will accompany the sports delegation on the Italian postal ship "Conte Verde" on June 26, departing from Shanghai and expected to arrive in Berlin, the capital of Germany, on July 22. They will depart from Germany with the delegation on September 4 and return to Shanghai on September 27. B. During the trip to Germany, they will pass through Hong Kong, Singapore, Colombo, Port Said, Venice in Italy, and then take a train directly to Berlin.

Participating in Assemblies: A. During the World Games, the German government has specially established the "International Sports Students Congress" and the World Leisure Discussion Congress to invite young people from various countries to participate and explore together in order to innovate and develop sports in the future. B. The leader of the delegation will review the qualifications of each member and assign them to participate in the above two types of assemblies. C. The International Sports Students Congress is scheduled to be held in Berlin from July 23 to August 17. D. The World Leisure Discussion Congress is scheduled to be held in Hamburg from July 23 to July 30. E. After the closing of the above two assemblies, the delegation will designate all or some of the members to inspect various places, depending on economic and time possibilities.

Fees: A. Various groups recommended by the Ministry of Education must pay a fee of 1,600 yuan in national currency before June 10. Any surplus will be refunded, and any deficiency must be paid. B. Members selected and subsidized by the Federation should pay a fee of 750 yuan in national currency for men and 1,200 yuan for women before June 1 (because the World Games does not invite women, the cost of staying in Germany is higher). If the payment is not made by the deadline, it will be considered a voluntary waiver. C. Self-funded members who are approved must pay a fee of 1,600 yuan in national currency for men and 2,000 yuan for women before June 10. Any surplus will be refunded, and any deficiency must be paid.

Preparation for Departure: A. After each member is selected or approved, they should immediately fill out the form prescribed by the Federation. B. If there are those who are waiting for the meeting at the ports passed by the Italian ship, they must declare it in advance, and their passports will be handled by themselves. C. If there are those who are staying in Germany or continuing to inspect Europe and will not return to the country with the delegation immediately, they must apply in advance to avoid losses, but the delegation will not be responsible for any accidents that occur during their stay in Europe. D. Members should submit twelve recent 2.5-inch photos. E. The delegation's uniform is a suit, with everyone wearing black clothes and white trousers. The upper body clothes will be made by the Federation to ensure uniformity. The length of the upper clothes should be sent to the Federation when paying the fee. The white trousers should be prepared by themselves.

Travel Tips: A. The climate in Germany is similar to that in central China in April and May, but the climate is very hot when passing through the Indian Ocean. B. For everyday clothes, do not wear light-colored clothes. Gray, black, and dark colors are more appropriate. C. Luggage should be lightweight and easy to carry. D. In addition to bringing a raincoat, everyone should also bring a swimsuit and rubber shoes for use on the ship and in Germany. E. The German government has specially prepared registered marks to facilitate the expenses of tourists from various countries. Members who wish to purchase and exchange these marks for personal use can submit them to the Federation for handling. The regulations for purchase, exchange, and use will be announced separately.

Municipal Education Bureau Stipulates Methods for Schools to Visit the Art Exhibition in Rotation 160

Also Approves Schools to Collect Visitation Fees Appropriately. Implements a Tense New Approach to Work

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday: "Approved per the National Children's Painting Exhibition's official letters No. 55 (Drawing) of April 18, 25th year [1936] and No. 83 (Drawing) of May 9th of the same year, regarding the children's art exhibition being held at the Municipal Sports Ground in the central district of Shanghai, considering that the distance from each school is different, it is requested to stipulate a rotational method for primary and secondary schools to visit, and to allow each school to appropriately collect visitation fees from students, limited to 20 cents in national currency, and so on." Upon approval, "We find that holding a children's art exhibition is an initiative for our country. Teachers and students of primary and secondary schools should enthusiastically visit to learn from it. We hereby stipulate the rotational method for primary and secondary schools to visit, which is attached, and allow schools to collect visitation fees from students when necessary, limited to 20 cents in national currency. The schedule lists schools that will visit on non-holidays, and schools are allowed to suspend classes. Schools in districts not listed may also visit freely. In addition to replying to the letters, we hereby make a public announcement."

Visitation Method

Attached: The rotational method for primary and secondary schools to visit the National Children's Art Exhibition is as follows: June 6th: all public and private primary and secondary schools in the central district, all municipal primary and secondary schools in the 2nd district of Shanghai South; June 7th: all public and private primary and secondary schools in the Jiangwan district, all municipal primary and secondary schools in the 1st district of Shanghai South; June 8th: all private primary and secondary schools in the 2nd district of Shanghai South; June 9th: all private primary and secondary schools in the 1st district of Shanghai South; June 10th: all municipal primary and secondary schools in the Zhabei district; June 11th: all private primary and secondary schools in the Zhabei district; June 12th: all municipal primary and secondary schools in the 2nd Special District; June 13th: all private primary and secondary schools in the 2nd Special District; June 14th: all private primary and secondary schools in the 1st Special District; June 15th: all municipal primary and secondary schools in the 1st Special District.

Arrangement Method

Since the establishment of the Arrangement and Design Committee for the National Children's Painting Exhibition, it has been working actively. The committee members, such as Chuan Boliang, Pan Gongwang, Zhou Xibao, and Zhu Fengming, all attend meetings on time and arrange the exhibition late into the night. The venue is the Municipal Sports Ground in the central district. It is estimated that over 40 large rooms will be needed to display the selected children's artworks and reference items from abroad. To pique the interest of visitors, the display methods in each room vary, using three-dimensional, wave-like, triangular, and stepped arrangements, etc. Each display room is decorated with various corresponding decorations, and the colors of the backing paper are also carefully coordinated to create an artistic atmosphere. All the supplies used, such as decorative paper, etc., are undertaken by the China Art Company, which makes them even more outstanding.

Commercial News

Strong Selling Sentiment in the Gold Market, Unable to Increase the Premium, Result Unchanged 166

The gold market was relatively stable yesterday due to the decline in the silver market and the rise in raw gold. However, as large dealers had high appetites, supply exceeded demand, and prices gradually fell back. However, the overall trend in the morning was very peaceful. Early in the morning, the overseas silver market reported that London was shrinking and the US was flat. It was said that after the close of trading, sellers were quoting 0.0625 lower than the posted price, but buyers were 0.125 lower, and no transactions were made. Forward silver prices shrank by 2 to 3 cents. Exchange rates rose slightly. London raw gold rose by 1 pence. The central bank's posted exchange rate remained unchanged for both British and American currencies, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The standard premium price was posted at 1135.7 yuan, and over-the-counter pre-market trading opened at 37.5 to 8 yuan. Dada, Yong, and others bought in, while Qingfa, Yongchun, Yuanyong, and others came out to offer, and the market fluctuated. The morning opening was high, and it remained stable because large dealers were still buying. However, sellers took advantage of the high prices and actively sold, making it difficult to sustain. The HSBC posted exchange rate was flat for both British and American currencies, and prices fell back again. However, as there were many buyers taking advantage of the low prices, the situation was maintained. Although the silver equalization tax shrank by 0.25, it rose slightly afterwards. However, there were still many people wanting to sell, and buyers were watching, resulting in a downstream close at noon. The swap premium remained at 3.1 yuan. The morning market situation is recorded below:

The opening price was 1137.7 yuan, up 0.6 yuan from the previous close. Although Yuanmao, Yongheng, and Chunyuanyong sold up to 7.6 yuan, Dadecheng and Dafayong went up to 7.8 yuan. Chunyuanyong, Fuxingyong, Dingkang, Tongyu, Runfu, Taiyong, and others gradually sold. Although the HSBC posted exchange rate was flat, it still fell to 3.2 yuan. Dadecheng and Huixianglai bought in. Popular Lecture

Ford (1863) 189

—Guo Xuan

Automobile Inventor

Who hasn't seen the beautiful cars displayed in the glass windows of large automobile companies? "Lincoln Zephyr," "Studebaker," "Buick"... they rush past on the asphalt roads with such style! Even the penniless poor have ridden in long-distance buses or public buses packed like canned goods, haven't they? The dust and the smell of gasoline are indeed unpleasant, but we can now travel in half a day distances that used to take two or three days by mule cart or donkey. How much convenience does this provide us? Especially in China, where railways are few, inland transportation relies almost entirely on this. Now the total length of highways in various provinces is approaching 100,000 kilometers, and we import automobiles worth tens of millions of yuan from abroad every year! Automobiles have truly become essential transportation tools!

Now, let me tell you the story of the automobile's invention:

Long ago, a Frenchman wanted to use machine power to drive a vehicle, but he didn't succeed. He only published his plan in a mechanical magazine. This magazine was seen by a young American worker across the Atlantic Ocean, who was deeply intrigued. He devoted himself to research, investing nearly ten years of effort and encountering countless setbacks. Finally, he built a practical automobile.

Who was this young man? He was Henry Ford, the famous American automobile tycoon of today.

Henry Ford was born in a small village outside the city of Troi in Michigan, USA. His father was a farmer who toiled his entire life and left him three thousand dollars when he died. But Ford had loved playing with machines since he was a child. In school, he loved the manual labor courses the most. So, as soon as he grew up, he immediately joined a steam engine company in Troi as an apprentice. He initially earned two dollars a week. The cost of living in America is very high, so that wasn't enough to support himself. He had to work a night job at a jewelry store, increasing his weekly income to four dollars, barely enough to make ends meet. At this time, he had to work fifteen hours a day, which was really exhausting. But he never forgot his research work. He was planning to start a clock company, planning to produce two thousand clocks every day, each costing 37.5 cents to make and selling for 40 cents on the market. Such a low-priced product would surely be welcomed, and his business would flourish. Most of his companions laughed at his delusion, so although a few people helped him, this ideal company never materialized. However, Ford always believed that if everything was produced in large quantities, it would reduce costs, lower prices, and thus gain a large market.

Because his plan couldn't be realized, Ford despondently returned home and rested for three years.

It was at this time that he read the article by the Frenchman, which deeply aroused his curiosity. He thought that if this kind of machine-powered vehicle could be made, it would be very popular and would greatly benefit society! So, from then on, he devoted himself to researching this invention.

A few dozen days later, he had already prepared a preliminary design, and he immediately went to Troi to buy materials. But on the way, he suddenly thought that if this kind of car could only be used by one or two people, like a bicycle, it wouldn't be anything special. It must be able to carry heavy loads and travel long distances. So, he thought about how to make the machine run more powerfully. He thought that trains were powered by steam, so this kind of car should also be powered by combustion. America produces kerosene, so why not try using kerosene?

From then on, he researched day and night at home. Because he didn't have advanced knowledge of electricity, the equipment for vaporizing and burning gasoline to generate electricity was never properly set up. Many relatives and friends advised him to stop this research to avoid wasting his career. We certainly know that all great inventors in the world have perseverance, and Ford was the same. So, not only did he not listen to others' advice, but he went to Troi to study electricity again.

He rejoined an electrical factory, working night shifts, earning only forty-five dollars a month. One day, the company bought a new machine, but none of the workers could start it. They had no choice but to abandon this great thing. Ford had been working in the factory for five months, and he had a considerable understanding of various machines. It just so happened that he passed by it, and a worker said, "Can you get it to work?" Ford said, "Let me try!" So, he inspected the various structures and felt that there was nothing new. As long as he stepped on it, it would start. He stepped on it with force, and sure enough, the machine started immediately. Because of this, Ford was highly trusted by the factory. His monthly salary increased to one hundred and fifty dollars.

He married a wife and bought a house. Next to the house, he built his own laboratory. He worked even harder to experiment with his ideal. Every day after work, he put on his oil-stained work clothes, grabbed a hammer, and went into his laboratory, banging away day and night. Everything comes down to focus. He improved and improved, worked and worked, and finally, one day, his ideal was about to be realized. It was already late at night, and his wife came several times to urge him to sleep, but he always said, "Don't rush me, it's just a little bit more!" So, the hammer rang again. Without realizing it, the long night had passed, and the morning sun had risen from the east. But at this time, Ford's carefully crafted first automobile was completed. Imagine how happy he must have been!

After breakfast, Ford drove this strange-looking car out. People on the road were stunned by this self-propelled monster. Ford just drove forward triumphantly. But when it was time to come back, the machine couldn't turn around. Ford was sweating profusely. The onlookers had to help him turn the car around. Of course, some people laughed at him, saying that he was simply crazy.

From the time Ford began researching and manufacturing automobiles to this time, it had been a full eight years, and he had only achieved this much. Although he hadn't reached complete success, Ford felt confident. Because things were too busy in the factory, and he couldn't spare time for manufacturing and research, he resigned from his factory job to focus on his own business. He still envisioned manufacturing automobiles on a large scale, selling them at low prices, just like the clock company he had dreamed of at the beginning. He immediately went around promoting his plan, seeking investment, believing that such a profitable business would surely attract money. But everyone thought his business was too risky, and no one was willing to invest a single cent!

Ford failed again!

At this time, there was a man named Willington who was also engaged in automobile manufacturing. However, his car was clumsier and larger than Ford's, but otherwise, they were roughly the same. Willington heard that Ford had succeeded and was afraid that Ford would get this profitable business, so he asked Ford for an automobile race.

Ford agreed to his request, and a date was set for the competition. That day, there was a huge crowd, all coming to see the novelty. Willington's car was tall and large, while Ford's car was small and shabby, which was unpleasant to look at. Everyone thought that Ford would definitely fail. At the sound of the command, the two strange cars started racing together. In less than half a li (里), Ford's car had already sprinted forward, leaving Willington far behind. Everyone couldn't help but cheer. Ford received a very warm welcome.

Ford hoped to take this opportunity to advertise to the merchants and realize his plan. But the cunning merchants wouldn't open their wallets until there was a real profit to be made, so Ford's goal still couldn't be achieved. Later, fortunately, a merchant named Couzens was the first to pay Ford a deposit to order the first automobile. This greatly encouraged Ford's courage. Just then, Willington asked for a race again, so Ford and Couzens drove the car and raced. As a result, Ford won again, and Willington had to admit defeat. And the hardworking Ford's luck started to improve from then on. Because of Ford's two victories and Couzens's promotion, merchants from all over America invested in Ford, and the company was established. Ford was the general manager, and his monthly salary was still one hundred and fifty dollars.

But this company soon went bankrupt because the shareholders wanted to make more money and conflicted with Ford's ideas. Ford had no capital, and he had a wife and children to feed. At this time, life was extremely difficult. Fortunately, his comrades Couzens and another man named Wills went bankrupt and came to help Ford. Ford hired only two workers, and he himself also wore workers' clothes and worked together with them. At that time, Ford's automobile was already famous, so there were many orders. Half a year later, the number of workers increased to forty. Ford didn't spend much on salaries besides supporting his family because his goal of large-scale production and low-price sales hadn't been achieved yet. Although his automobiles now sold for only nine hundred dollars each, that was already twice as cheap as others' cars.

That winter, the holiday season for settling accounts arrived. Because the market was bad at the time, Ford had bad luck again, and the company lost money and couldn't survive. On that New Year's Day, Ford cried bitterly to the workers, explaining the situation of bankruptcy and expressing his plans and hopes. The workers were very moved and were willing to continue without pay. Ford felt both happy and frustrated. Just then, the European War (Germany and various countries went to war) broke out, and the demand for automobiles greatly increased. Ford's business greatly prospered. Later, the number of workers increased to 16,000. Because Ford was a worker himself, he knew the hardships of labor and was the first to implement the eight-hour workday, breaking the ten-hour workday in American factories. He also increased the wages of workers, with a minimum daily wage of five dollars (equivalent to 17 or 18 yuan in Chinese currency). Factory owners in various countries were astonished, but Ford's business only continued to develop.

At this time, Ford had fully realized his ideal of large-scale production and low-price sales. His hard work had finally paid off!

Today, Ford has become a great American tycoon, with his wealth approaching one hundred million gold dollars. But he has indeed created happiness for many poor workers. There are more than tens of thousands of workers in his factories. Making an automobile requires 7,882 steps. We can imagine how many people are employed. He has set up hospitals, schools, and various sanitation facilities for workers, and he also gives workers bonuses from annual profits. We say that Ford has not only benefited mankind, giving us convenient transportation tools, but can also be said to be a great social revolutionary!

John A. Brashear 190

— Zhao Yahao

Chinese artisans who manufacture gemstone crystal possess high skills, but they only create ornaments for ladies and young women. Foreign artisans, however, can use their skills to discover the secrets of the universe and create human happiness. Zhuangzi said: "If you can safeguard the One, what can be lost? Some use it to dominate, while others cannot escape being adrift and sinking."

(Editor)

Brashear was an American, born in Pittsburgh. He was affable and liked making friends. He often told people, "The value of a person's life depends on the number of friends he makes, and a person's energy should be used to benefit others." He once traveled to China. In his speeches, he often praised China and was very concerned about Chinese education, especially advocating for the establishment of schools for the blind in China.

When he was young, he liked observing celestial bodies. He believed that our eyes cannot see stars that are very far away, so he always wanted to make a tool to penetrate the secrets of space. Indeed, he got an excellent opportunity: when he was eight years old, a man brought a telescope and traveled to his village. He liked it so much that he immediately rented the telescope from the man to take a look at the celestial phenomena. At that time, he felt that the marvels of creation had to be deeply understood. It made him reluctant to sleep every night, pacing around the village with his head raised, paying attention to the arrangement of the stars in the sky. He often told people, "When I grow up, I must study astronomy." He was only eight years old, but he already had the ambition to create happiness for mankind. This is so worthy of our attention!

However, he was born into a poor family and did not have the means to pursue advanced studies. After graduating from middle school, he served in society. At first, he was an apprentice, and three years later he became a moderately experienced mechanic. At the age of twenty, he worked as a low-level mechanic in a steel factory in Pittsburgh. He spent twenty-one years immersed in coal smoke and iron filings.

Comparing his living situation with that of poor Chinese people in China, it can be said that they were equally difficult. However, his spirit is enough to make us admire him. Apart from the time he spent working in the factory, his closest friends were old books and magazines. He studied diligently, sowing the seeds for creating happiness for mankind. He especially paid attention to the phenomena in the sky, so he often looked at the scenery of the sky outside the window on the tram on his way to work and back home. Sometimes, after lunch, he gathered a large group of fellow workers together to chat. During their conversations, he often introduced them to knowledge about the sky. He was also so enthusiastic about worker education.

At the age of twenty-one, he married Phoebe, who was also a very knowledgeable woman, so they were able to help each other in their research. His success was greatly helped by her. He wanted to build a house, but because his income was not high, he had to do it himself. So after work, he would go back to help her build the house. It took them about a year to build this house.

Soon after she lived with him, she was influenced by his concern for astrology. Their wish was to make their own telescope, so his house gradually became a small factory. Most of the tools he used were made by himself. From then on, they began to grind a piece of glass, working hard day and night. It took them three years to finish grinding the glass piece in the telescope. Truly, even though it is just a piece of glass, grinding it into something that can be used in a telescope is not an easy task! Because if the glass is not spherical or parabolic in curvature, it cannot be used to observe celestial bodies. If there is even a slight mark on the glass, the observation of celestial bodies will be greatly affected. After he ground this piece of glass, he immediately took it to the Pittsburgh Observatory to see Mr. Langley and asked him to teach him how to install it in the telescope tube. Soon, his self-made telescope was successful. He cut a hole in the roof of his house and extended the telescope out. Ah! The vastness of the sky was already in his grasp. Three years of work were completed in one day. How happy they were! That night, happiness overcame fatigue and sleepiness, and they observed through this telescope for an entire night. The next day, he invited many friends, villagers, and fellow workers to share the joy of exploring the mysterious space. Although his telescope was simple, his wish was considered a success. This telescope was only five inches in diameter, and what it could see in the sky could not satisfy this enterprising scientist, so he decided to make an even bigger one.

Later, they ground another piece of glass, twelve inches in diameter. It took another two years. After grinding it, he wanted to apply a thin layer of silver on the glass to reflect strong light. Unfortunately, when he was applying the silver, the glass suddenly broke. This major blow simply stunned him. That day, when he was working in the factory, he looked like a fool. After work, he returned to his home, but he could not find Mrs. Phoebe in the house or in the kitchen. Finally, he found her in his own workshop, where she was starting a fire. At that time, the water in the steam pot was boiling, and a new piece of glass had been installed on his glass grinding machine. She smiled at him and said, "Let's not be discouraged. We just need to make another one, and it has to be better than the broken one." These words seemed to pour oil on the dying embers, reigniting the scientist's vigorous courage. Sure enough, soon they completed an even better piece of glass.

This twelve-inch diameter glass was about the same size as the ones used in famous universities in America. However, its function was even greater! He used his free time to observe the changing phenomena in space through this telescope. At this time, newspapers often published his works, and his success attracted even more attention.

He worked in the factory for twenty-one years. Later, he was hired by the University of Pittsburgh as a professor of astronomy. Ah! It is so rare and honorable for an ordinary mechanic to be promoted to a professor at a university! Later, he even became the president of the University of Pittsburgh. This was nothing more than the result of his hard work. From then on, his genius could be fully developed. At the same time, he opened a factory specializing in the manufacture of astronomical instruments.

There is an American Society of Mechanical Engineers, which is a world-renowned engineering society. He also served as the president of this society, and he was the most admired president.

Grinding glass for astronomical telescopes became his specialty. Because the larger the circumference or the larger the diameter of the glass, the more difficult the grinding process becomes. If there were a six-foot diameter, two-ton glass lens, it would be almost impossible to do it by hand. Now the telescope at the Mount Wilson Observatory (six feet in diameter, weighing over two tons) is the crystallization of this scientist's hard work.

In science, the most common unit for measuring length is the meter. But how long is a meter exactly? Scientists want to create a "standard meter ruler" made of platinum-iridium alloy. But before creating the standard ruler, one must know how to determine the length of the standard meter ruler. Scientists want to use the wavelength of light as the standard. But to calculate how many wavelengths of light are equal to one meter, one must use an accurate lens, which is flat, but its degree of "flatness" cannot be off by more than one millionth of an inch (10 inches) from the ideal plane. This is very difficult. The International Bureau of Weights and Measures sought someone to grind this glass, and this scientist was selected and completed this piece of glass.
